\documentclass[11pt]{article}

    
    
    \usepackage[T1]{fontenc}
    % Nicer default font (+ math font) than Computer Modern for most use cases
    \usepackage{mathpazo}

    % Basic figure setup, for now with no caption control since it's done
    % automatically by Pandoc (which extracts ![](path) syntax from Markdown).
    \usepackage{graphicx}
    % We will generate all images so they have a width \maxwidth. This means
    % that they will get their normal width if they fit onto the page, but
    % are scaled down if they would overflow the margins.
    \makeatletter
    \def\maxwidth{\ifdim\Gin@nat@width>\linewidth\linewidth
    \else\Gin@nat@width\fi}
    \makeatother
    \let\Oldincludegraphics\includegraphics
    % Set max figure width to be 80% of text width, for now hardcoded.
    \renewcommand{\includegraphics}[1]{\Oldincludegraphics[width=.8\maxwidth]{#1}}
    % Ensure that by default, figures have no caption (until we provide a
    % proper Figure object with a Caption API and a way to capture that
    % in the conversion process - todo).
    \usepackage{caption}
    \DeclareCaptionLabelFormat{nolabel}{}
    \captionsetup{labelformat=nolabel}

    \usepackage{adjustbox} % Used to constrain images to a maximum size 
    \usepackage{xcolor} % Allow colors to be defined
    \usepackage{enumerate} % Needed for markdown enumerations to work
    \usepackage{geometry} % Used to adjust the document margins
    \usepackage{amsmath} % Equations
    \usepackage{amssymb} % Equations
    \usepackage{textcomp} % defines textquotesingle
    % Hack from http://tex.stackexchange.com/a/47451/13684:
    \AtBeginDocument{%
        \def\PYZsq{\textquotesingle}% Upright quotes in Pygmentized code
    }
    \usepackage{upquote} % Upright quotes for verbatim code
    \usepackage{eurosym} % defines \euro
    \usepackage[mathletters]{ucs} % Extended unicode (utf-8) support
    \usepackage[utf8x]{inputenc} % Allow utf-8 characters in the tex document
    \usepackage{fancyvrb} % verbatim replacement that allows latex
    \usepackage{grffile} % extends the file name processing of package graphics 
                         % to support a larger range

    % internal navigation ('pdf bookmarks' for the table of contents,

    \usepackage[inline]{enumitem} % IRkernel/repr support (it uses the enumerate* environment)
    \usepackage[normalem]{ulem} % ulem is needed to support strikethroughs (\sout)
                                % normalem makes italics be italics, not underlines

\def\PY@reset{\let\PY@it=\relax \let\PY@bf=\relax%
    \let\PY@ul=\relax \let\PY@tc=\relax%
    \let\PY@bc=\relax \let\PY@ff=\relax}
\def\PY@tok#1{\csname PY@tok@#1\endcsname}
\def\PY@toks#1+{\ifx\relax#1\empty\else%
    \PY@tok{#1}\expandafter\PY@toks\fi}
\def\PY@do#1{\PY@bc{\PY@tc{\PY@ul{%
    \PY@it{\PY@bf{\PY@ff{#1}}}}}}}
\def\PY#1#2{\PY@reset\PY@toks#1+\relax+\PY@do{#2}}

    \hypertarget{systems-check}{%
\subsection{Systems check}\label{systems-check}}

Do you have a working Python installation, with the \texttt{pandas}
package ?

    \textbf{Note :} This cell should run without raising a traceback.
Assuming it runs, you can also try printing the value of
\texttt{pd.\_\_version\_\_} to see what version of \texttt{pandas} you
have installed.

    \hypertarget{general-syntax}{%
\subsection{04. General Syntax}\label{general-syntax}}

    \textbf{0401} \texttt{Creating\ a\ main\ script}

    \begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
{\color{incolor}In [{\color{incolor}6}]:} \PY{k}{def} \PY{n+nf}{main}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
            \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{This is the syntax.py file.}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
        
        \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Allows running script with functions in any order.}
        \PY{k}{if} \PY{n+nv+vm}{\PYZus{}\PYZus{}name\PYZus{}\PYZus{}} \PY{o}{==} \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZus{}\PYZus{}main\PYZus{}\PYZus{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{:} \PY{n}{main}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}
\end{Verbatim}


    \begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
This is the syntax.py file.

    \end{Verbatim}

    \textbf{0402} \texttt{Understanding\ whitespace\ in\ Python}

    \begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
{\color{incolor}In [{\color{incolor}9}]:} \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Indentation tells python how the code is associated.}
        \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Spacing has to be consistent.}
        \PY{k}{def} \PY{n+nf}{main}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
            \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{This is the syntax.py file.}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{k}{if} \PY{n+nv+vm}{\PYZus{}\PYZus{}name\PYZus{}\PYZus{}} \PY{o}{==} \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZus{}\PYZus{}main\PYZus{}\PYZus{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{:} \PY{n}{main}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}
\end{Verbatim}


    \begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
This is the syntax.py file.

    \end{Verbatim}

    \textbf{0403} \texttt{Commenting\ code}

    \begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
{\color{incolor}In [{\color{incolor}11}]:} \PY{c+ch}{\PYZsh{}!/usr/bin/python3}
         \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} comments.py by Bill Weinman [http://bw.org/]}
         \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} This is an exercise file from Python 3 Essential Training on lynda.com}
         \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Copyright 2010 The BearHeart Group, LLC}
         
         \PY{k}{def} \PY{n+nf}{main}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
             \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{n} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{primes}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
                 \PY{k}{if} \PY{n}{n} \PY{o}{\PYZgt{}} \PY{l+m+mi}{100}\PY{p}{:} \PY{k}{break}
                 \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{n}\PY{p}{)}
         
         \PY{k}{def} \PY{n+nf}{isprime}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{n}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
             \PY{k}{if} \PY{n}{n} \PY{o}{==} \PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{:} \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} one is never prime}
                 \PY{k}{return} \PY{k+kc}{False}
             \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{x} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n+nb}{range}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{2}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{n}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
                 \PY{k}{if} \PY{n}{n} \PY{o}{\PYZpc{}} \PY{n}{x} \PY{o}{==} \PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{:}
                     \PY{k}{return} \PY{k+kc}{False} \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} found a divisor not prime}
             \PY{k}{else}\PY{p}{:}
                 \PY{k}{return} \PY{k+kc}{True}
         
         \PY{k}{def} \PY{n+nf}{primes}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{n} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
            \PY{k}{while}\PY{p}{(}\PY{k+kc}{True}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
                \PY{k}{if} \PY{n}{isprime}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{n}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:} \PY{k}{yield} \PY{n}{n} \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} yield makes this a generator}
                \PY{n}{n} \PY{o}{+}\PY{o}{=} \PY{l+m+mi}{1} 
         
         \PY{k}{if} \PY{n+nv+vm}{\PYZus{}\PYZus{}name\PYZus{}\PYZus{}} \PY{o}{==} \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZus{}\PYZus{}main\PYZus{}\PYZus{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{:} \PY{n}{main}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}
\end{Verbatim}

    \hypertarget{variables-objects-and-values}{%
\subsection{05. Variables Objects and
Values}\label{variables-objects-and-values}}

    \textbf{0501}
\texttt{Understanding\ variables\ and\ objects\ in\ Python}

    \begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
{\color{incolor}In [{\color{incolor}12}]:} \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} all variables in python are first class objects.}
         \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} what looks like a simple variable may be something more complex.}
         \PY{n}{x} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+m+mi}{42}
         \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{x}\PY{p}{)}
         \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb}{id}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{x}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
         \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb}{type}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{x}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
\end{Verbatim}


    \begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
42
1841849856
<class 'int'>

    \end{Verbatim}

    \textbf{0502} \texttt{Distinguishing\ mutable\ and\ immutable\ objects}

    \begin{itemize}
\tightlist
\item
  ** Objects in Python may be mutable or immutable **
\item
  ** Mutable objects may change value, immutable objects may not **
\end{itemize}

    \begin{itemize}
\tightlist
\item
  May look like it's value changes.
\item
  Distinction is visible using id()
\item
  Container objects (tuples, lists, etc) may appear to chage value
\end{itemize}

    \begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
{\color{incolor}In [{\color{incolor}2}]:} \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Change variable to refer to a different object.}
        \PY{n}{x} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+m+mi}{42}
        \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{x}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb}{id}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{x}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{n}{x} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+m+mi}{43}
        \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{x}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb}{id}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{x}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{n}{x} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+m+mi}{42}
        \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{x}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb}{id}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{x}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)} \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} id is now original value}
\end{Verbatim}


    \begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
42
1841849856
43
1841849888
42
1841849856

    \end{Verbatim}

    \begin{itemize}
\tightlist
\item
  ** Most fundamental types in Python are immutable. **
\item
  numbers, strings, tuples
\item
  ** Mutable objects include **
\item
  lists, dictionaries, other objects depending upon implementation
\end{itemize}

    \textbf{0503} \texttt{Using\ numbers}

    \begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
{\color{incolor}In [{\color{incolor}14}]:} \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} The \PYZpc{} (modulo) operator yields the remainder from the division }
         \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} of the first argument by the second. The numeric arguments are }
         \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} first converted to a common type. A zero right argument raises }
         \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} the ZeroDivisionError exception. The arguments may be floating }
         \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} point numbers, e.g., 3.14\PYZpc{}0.7 equals 0.34 (since 3.14 equals 4*0.7 + 0.34.) }
         \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} The modulo operator always yields a result with the same sign as its second }
         \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} operand (or zero); the absolute value of the result is strictly smaller than }
         \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} the absolute value of the second operand.}
         
         \PY{k}{def} \PY{n+nf}{main}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
             
             \PY{n}{num} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+m+mi}{42}
             \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{num}\PY{p}{)}
             \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb}{type}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{num}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{num}\PY{p}{)}
             
             \PY{n}{n} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+m+mf}{42.0}
             \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{n}\PY{p}{)}
             \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb}{type}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{n}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{n}\PY{p}{)}
             
             \PY{n}{x} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+m+mi}{42} \PY{o}{/} \PY{l+m+mi}{9}
             \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{x}\PY{p}{)}
             \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb}{type}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{x}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{x}\PY{p}{)}
             
             \PY{n}{i} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+m+mi}{42} \PY{o}{/}\PY{o}{/} \PY{l+m+mi}{9} \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}integer division not rounded up}
             \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{i}\PY{p}{)}
             \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb}{type}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{i}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{i}\PY{p}{)}
             
             \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} rounded = round(42 / 9) }
             \PY{n}{rounded} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb}{round}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{42} \PY{o}{/} \PY{l+m+mi}{9}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{2}\PY{p}{)} \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}how many digits}
             \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{rounded}\PY{p}{)}
             \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb}{type}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{rounded}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{rounded}\PY{p}{)}
             
             \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} modula}
             \PY{n}{remainder} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+m+mi}{42} \PY{o}{\PYZpc{}} \PY{l+m+mi}{9}
             \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{remainder}\PY{p}{)}
             \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb}{type}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{remainder}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{remainder}\PY{p}{)}
             
             \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} ensure int}
             \PY{n}{num} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb}{int}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mf}{42.9}\PY{p}{)}
             \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb}{type}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{num}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{num}\PY{p}{)}
             
             \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} ensure float}
             \PY{n}{num} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb}{float}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mf}{42.9}\PY{p}{)}
             \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb}{type}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{num}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{num}\PY{p}{)}
         
         \PY{k}{if} \PY{n+nv+vm}{\PYZus{}\PYZus{}name\PYZus{}\PYZus{}} \PY{o}{==} \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZus{}\PYZus{}main\PYZus{}\PYZus{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{:} \PY{n}{main}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}

    \textbf{0504} \texttt{Using\ strings}

    \textbf{0701} \texttt{Creating\ loops\ with\ while}

    \begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]

         \PY{k}{def} \PY{n+nf}{main}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
             \PY{n}{a}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{b} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{1}

                 \PY{n}{a}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{b} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{b}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{a} \PY{o}{+} \PY{n}{b}
         
         \PY{k}{if} \PY{n+nv+vm}{\PYZus{}\PYZus{}name\PYZus{}\PYZus{}} \PY{o}{==} \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZus{}\PYZus{}main\PYZus{}\PYZus{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{:} \PY{n}{main}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}

    \textbf{0702} \texttt{Iterating\ with\ for}

    \begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
{\color{incolor}In [{\color{incolor}25}]:} \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} The for loop is the most common because }
         \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} so many objects in Python are iterators.}
         \PY{k}{def} \PY{n+nf}{main}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
             \PY{n}{fh} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb}{open}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{lines.txt}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}
             
             \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{line} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{fh}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{readlines}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:} \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} iterator}
                 \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{line}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{end}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)} \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} remove newline}
                 
             \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{line} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{2}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{3}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{4}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{5}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{:} \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} iterator}
                 \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{line}\PY{p}{)} \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} remove newline}
                 
             \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{line} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{string}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{:} \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} iterator}

         \PY{n+nb}{list}\PY{p}{[}\PY{p}{:}\PY{p}{]} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb}{range}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{100}\PY{p}{)}
         \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb}{list}\PY{p}{)}
         \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb}{list}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{27}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{)}
         \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb}{list}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{27}\PY{p}{:}\PY{l+m+mi}{42}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{)}
         \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb}{list}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{27}\PY{p}{:}\PY{l+m+mi}{42}\PY{p}{:}\PY{l+m+mi}{3}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{)} \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} slice get every third element, step argument}
         
         \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{i} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n+nb}{list}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{27}\PY{p}{:}\PY{l+m+mi}{43}\PY{p}{:}\PY{l+m+mi}{3}\PY{p}{]} \PY{p}{:} \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{i}\PY{p}{)}
             
         \PY{n+nb}{list}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{27}\PY{p}{:}\PY{l+m+mi}{43}\PY{p}{:}\PY{l+m+mi}{3}\PY{p}{]} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{99}\PY{p}{,}\PY{l+m+mi}{99}\PY{p}{,}\PY{l+m+mi}{99}\PY{p}{,}\PY{l+m+mi}{99}\PY{p}{,}\PY{l+m+mi}{99}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{99}\PY{p}{)} \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} assign to slice}
         \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb}{list}\PY{p}{)}
\end{Verbatim}

    \textbf{0806} \texttt{Understanding\ operator\ precedence}

    \begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
{\color{incolor}In [{\color{incolor}83}]:} \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Which operations get evaluated first}
         \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Multiplacation/Division have higher precedence than Addition/Subtraction}
         
         \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} 1. 5 * 25 = 125}
         \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} 2. 14 / 2 = 7}
         \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} 3. 125 + 7 = 132}
         \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{5} \PY{o}{*} \PY{l+m+mi}{25} \PY{o}{+} \PY{l+m+mi}{14} \PY{o}{/} \PY{l+m+mi}{2}\PY{p}{)}
         
         \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Get different result}
         \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} 1. 25 + 14 = 39}
         \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} 2. 39 / 2 = 19.5}
         \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} 3. 19.5 * 5 = 97.5}
         \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{5} \PY{o}{*} \PY{p}{(} \PY{l+m+mi}{25} \PY{o}{+} \PY{l+m+mi}{14} \PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{/} \PY{l+m+mi}{2}\PY{p}{)}
\end{Verbatim}


    \begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
132.0
97.5

    \end{Verbatim}

    \hypertarget{regular-expressions}{%
\subsection{09. Regular Expressions}\label{regular-expressions}}

    \textbf{0901} \texttt{Using\ Regular\ Expression}

    \begin{itemize}
\tightlist
\item
  Regular expressions are a very powerfull method of matching patterns
  in text.
\item
  Actually a small language in itself, regexes can be very simple or
  complex
\item
  Implemented in Python with the ``re'' module
\end{itemize}

    \begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
{\color{incolor}In [{\color{incolor}86}]:} \PY{k+kn}{import} \PY{n+nn}{re}
         \PY{n}{pattern} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{re}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{compile}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{r}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZbs{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{d}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZbs{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{d}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZbs{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{d}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}
         \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} if re.search(regex, line): print(line)}
\end{Verbatim}


    \textbf{0902} \texttt{Searching\ with\ regular\ expressions}

    \begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
{\color{incolor}In [{\color{incolor}3}]:} \PY{k+kn}{import} \PY{n+nn}{re}
        
        \PY{k}{def} \PY{n+nf}{main}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
            \PY{n}{fh} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb}{open}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{raven.txt}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}
            \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{line} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{fh}\PY{p}{:}
                \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} look for lenore or nevermore}
                \PY{k}{if} \PY{n}{re}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{search}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{(Len|Neverm)ore}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{line}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
                    \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{line}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{end}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}
                    
                \PY{n}{match} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{re}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{search}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{(Len|Neverm)ore}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{line}\PY{p}{)}
                \PY{k}{if} \PY{n}{match}\PY{p}{:}
                    \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{match}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{group}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
        
        \PY{k}{if} \PY{n+nv+vm}{\PYZus{}\PYZus{}name\PYZus{}\PYZus{}} \PY{o}{==} \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZus{}\PYZus{}main\PYZus{}\PYZus{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{:} \PY{n}{main}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}
\end{Verbatim}

    \textbf{0903} \texttt{Replacing\ with\ regular\ expressions}

    \begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
{\color{incolor}In [{\color{incolor}9}]:} \PY{k+kn}{import} \PY{n+nn}{re}
        
        \PY{k}{def} \PY{n+nf}{main}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
            \PY{n}{fh} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb}{open}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{raven.txt}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}
            \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}for line in fh:}
                \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}print(re.sub(\PYZsq{}(Len|Neverm)ore\PYZsq{}, \PYZsq{}\PYZsh{}\PYZsh{}\PYZsh{}\PYZsq{}, line), end=\PYZsq{}\PYZsq{})}
        
            \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{line} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{fh}\PY{p}{:}
                \PY{n}{match} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{re}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{search}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{(Len|Neverm)ore}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{line}\PY{p}{)}
                \PY{k}{if} \PY{n}{match}\PY{p}{:}
                    \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{line}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{replace}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{match}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{group}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsh{}\PYZsh{}\PYZsh{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{end}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}
        
        \PY{k}{if} \PY{n+nv+vm}{\PYZus{}\PYZus{}name\PYZus{}\PYZus{}} \PY{o}{==} \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZus{}\PYZus{}main\PYZus{}\PYZus{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{:} \PY{n}{main}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}
\end{Verbatim}

    \textbf{0904} \texttt{Reusing\ regular\ expressions\ with\ re.compile}

    \begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
{\color{incolor}In [{\color{incolor}14}]:} \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Pre\PYZhy{}compile pattern for efficiency}
         \PY{k+kn}{import} \PY{n+nn}{re}
         
         \PY{k}{def} \PY{n+nf}{main}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
             \PY{n}{fh} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb}{open}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{raven.txt}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}
             \PY{n}{pattern} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{re}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{compile}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{(Len|Neverm)ore}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{re}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{IGNORECASE}\PY{p}{)}
             \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{line} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{fh}\PY{p}{:}
                 \PY{k}{if} \PY{n}{re}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{search}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{pattern}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{line}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
                     \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} print(line, end=\PYZsq{}\PYZsq{})}
                     \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{pattern}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{sub}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsh{}\PYZsh{}\PYZsh{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{line}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{end}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}
         
         \PY{k}{if} \PY{n+nv+vm}{\PYZus{}\PYZus{}name\PYZus{}\PYZus{}} \PY{o}{==} \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZus{}\PYZus{}main\PYZus{}\PYZus{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{:} \PY{n}{main}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}

    \hypertarget{exceptions}{%
\subsection{10. Exceptions}\label{exceptions}}

    \textbf{1001} \texttt{Learning\ how\ exceptions\ work}

    \begin{itemize}
\tightlist
\item
  Exceptions are the key method of handlinf errors in Python
\item
  ``try'' something, then catch an exception with ``except''
\item
  You may raise your own exceptions with ``raise''
\end{itemize}

    \textbf{1002} \texttt{Handling\ exceptions}

    \begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
{\color{incolor}In [{\color{incolor}28}]:} \PY{k}{def} \PY{n+nf}{main}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
             \PY{k}{try}\PY{p}{:} 
                 \PY{n}{fh} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb}{open}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{xlines.txt}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}
             \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} except: \PYZsh{} catch any error}
             \PY{k}{except} \PY{n+ne}{IOError} \PY{k}{as} \PY{n}{e}\PY{p}{:}
                 \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{could not open the file:}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{e}\PY{p}{)}
             \PY{k}{else}\PY{p}{:} 
                 \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{line} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{fh}\PY{p}{:} \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{line}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{strip}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
         
         \PY{k}{if} \PY{n+nv+vm}{\PYZus{}\PYZus{}name\PYZus{}\PYZus{}} \PY{o}{==} \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZus{}\PYZus{}main\PYZus{}\PYZus{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{:} \PY{n}{main}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}
\end{Verbatim}


    \begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
could not open the file: [Errno 2] No such file or directory: 'xlines.doc'

    \end{Verbatim}

    \textbf{1003} \texttt{Raising\ exceptions}

    \begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
{\color{incolor}In [{\color{incolor}29}]:} \PY{k}{def} \PY{n+nf}{main}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
             \PY{k}{try}\PY{p}{:} 
                 \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{line} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{readfile}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{lines.doc}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:} \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{line}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{strip}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
             \PY{k}{except} \PY{n+ne}{IOError} \PY{k}{as} \PY{n}{e}\PY{p}{:}
                 \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{cannot read file:}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{e}\PY{p}{)}
             \PY{k}{except} \PY{n+ne}{ValueError} \PY{k}{as} \PY{n}{e}\PY{p}{:}
                 \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{bad filename:}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{e}\PY{p}{)}
                 
         \PY{k}{def} \PY{n+nf}{readfile}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{filename}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
             \PY{k}{if} \PY{n}{filename}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{endswith}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{.txt}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
                 \PY{n}{fh} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb}{open}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{filename}\PY{p}{)}
                 \PY{k}{return} \PY{n}{fh}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{readlines}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}
             \PY{k}{else}\PY{p}{:} \PY{k}{raise} \PY{n+ne}{ValueError}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{Filename must end with .txt}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}
         
         \PY{k}{if} \PY{n+nv+vm}{\PYZus{}\PYZus{}name\PYZus{}\PYZus{}} \PY{o}{==} \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZus{}\PYZus{}main\PYZus{}\PYZus{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{:} \PY{n}{main}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}
\end{Verbatim}

    \textbf{1102} \texttt{Using\ lists\ of\ arguments}

    \begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]

{\color{incolor}In [{\color{incolor}126}]:} \PY{k}{class} \PY{n+nc}{inclusive\PYZus{}range}\PY{p}{:}
              
              \PY{k}{def} \PY{n+nf}{\PYZus{}\PYZus{}init\PYZus{}\PYZus{}}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{p}{,} \PY{o}{*}\PY{n}{args}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
                  \PY{n}{numargs} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb}{len}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{args}\PY{p}{)}
                  \PY{k}{if} \PY{n}{numargs} \PY{o}{\PYZlt{}} \PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{:} \PY{k}{raise} \PY{n+ne}{TypeError}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{requires atleast one argument}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}
                  \PY{k}{elif} \PY{n}{numargs} \PY{o}{==} \PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{:}
                      \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{stop} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{args}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{]}
                      \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{start} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+m+mi}{0}
                      \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{step} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+m+mi}{1}
                  \PY{k}{elif} \PY{n}{numargs} \PY{o}{==} \PY{l+m+mi}{2}\PY{p}{:}
                      \PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{start}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{stop}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{args}
                      \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{step} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+m+mi}{1}
                  \PY{k}{elif} \PY{n}{numargs} \PY{o}{==} \PY{l+m+mi}{3}\PY{p}{:}
                      \PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{start}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{stop}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{step}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{args}
                  \PY{k}{else}\PY{p}{:} \PY{k}{raise} \PY{n+ne}{TypeError}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{expected at most 3 arguments, got }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{format}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{numargs}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
              
              \PY{k}{def} \PY{n+nf}{\PYZus{}\PYZus{}iter\PYZus{}\PYZus{}}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
                  \PY{n}{i} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{start}
                  \PY{k}{while} \PY{n}{i} \PY{o}{\PYZlt{}}\PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{stop}\PY{p}{:}
                      \PY{k}{yield} \PY{n}{i}
                      \PY{n}{i} \PY{o}{+}\PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{step}
          
          \PY{k}{def} \PY{n+nf}{main}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
              \PY{n}{o} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{inclusive\PYZus{}range}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{5}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{25}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{7}\PY{p}{)} \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} start, stop, step}
              \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{i} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{o}\PY{p}{:} \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{i}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{end} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{ }\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}

             \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{        This is a string        }\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{rstrip}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
             \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{This is a fun new string}\PY{l+s+se}{\PYZbs{}n}\PY{l+s+se}{\PYZbs{}n}\PY{l+s+se}{\PYZbs{}n}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{rstrip}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+se}{\PYZbs{}n}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
             \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{s}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{isalnum}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)} 
             \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{s}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{isalpha}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
             \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{s}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{isdigit}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
             \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{s}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{isprintable}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
         
         \PY{k}{if} \PY{n+nv+vm}{\PYZus{}\PYZus{}name\PYZus{}\PYZus{}} \PY{o}{==} \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZus{}\PYZus{}main\PYZus{}\PYZus{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{:} \PY{n}{main}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}

    \textbf{1403} \texttt{Organizing\ data\ with\ dictionaries}

              infile = open(\PYZsq{}lines.txt\PYZsq{}, \PYZsq{}r\PYZsq{})
              outfile = open(\PYZsq{}new.txt\PYZsq{}, \PYZsq{}w\PYZsq{})
              for line in infile:
                  print(line, file = outfile, end = \PYZsq{}\PYZsq{})
              print(\PYZsq{}Done\PYZsq{})
              
              buffersize = 50000
              infile = open(\PYZsq{}bigfile.txt\PYZsq{}, \PYZsq{}r\PYZsq{})
              outfile = open(\PYZsq{}newbigfile.txt\PYZsq{}, \PYZsq{}w\PYZsq{})
              buffer = infile.read(buffersize)
              while len(buffer):
                  outfile.write(buffer)
                  print(\PYZsq{}.\PYZsq{}, end=\PYZsq{}\PYZsq{})
                  buffer = infile.read(buffersize)
              print(\PYZsq{}Done\PYZsq{})

             \PY{n}{db}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{update}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb}{dict}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{t1} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{three}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{i1} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+m+mi}{103}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
             \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{row} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{db}\PY{p}{:} \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{row}\PY{p}{)}
         
             \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{Delete rows}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}

                 \PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{tens}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{:} \PY{p}{(}
                     \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{ten}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{twenty}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{thirty}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{forty}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{fifty}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{sixty}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{seventy}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{eighty}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{ninety}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}
                 \PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{teens}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{:} \PY{p}{(}

                 \PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{quarters}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{:} \PY{p}{(}
                     \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{o}\PY{l+s+se}{\PYZbs{}\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{clock}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{quarter}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{half}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}
                 \PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{range}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{:} \PY{p}{\PYZob{}}
                     \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{hundred}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{:} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{hundred}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}
                 \PY{p}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{misc}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{:} \PY{p}{\PYZob{}}
                     \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{minus}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{:} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{minus}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}
                 \PY{p}{\PYZcb{}}
             \PY{p}{\PYZcb{}}
             \PY{n}{\PYZus{}oor} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{OOR}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}    \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Out Of Range}
         
             \PY{k}{def} \PY{n+nf}{\PYZus{}\PYZus{}init\PYZus{}\PYZus{}}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{n}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
                 \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{\PYZus{}\PYZus{}number} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{n}\PY{p}{;}
         
             \PY{k}{def} \PY{n+nf}{numwords}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{num} \PY{o}{=} \PY{k+kc}{None}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
                 \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{Return the number as words}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}
                 \PY{n}{n} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{\PYZus{}\PYZus{}number} \PY{k}{if} \PY{n}{num} \PY{o+ow}{is} \PY{k+kc}{None} \PY{k}{else} \PY{n}{num}
                 \PY{n}{s} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}
                 \PY{k}{if} \PY{n}{n} \PY{o}{\PYZlt{}} \PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{:}           \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} negative numbers}
                     \PY{n}{s} \PY{o}{+}\PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{\PYZus{}words}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{misc}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{minus}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{]} \PY{o}{+} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{ }\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}
                     \PY{n}{n} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb}{abs}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{n}\PY{p}{)}
                 \PY{k}{if} \PY{n}{n} \PY{o}{\PYZlt{}} \PY{l+m+mi}{10}\PY{p}{:}          \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} single\PYZhy{}digit numbers}
                     \PY{n}{s} \PY{o}{+}\PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{\PYZus{}words}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{ones}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{n}\PY{p}{]}  
                 \PY{k}{elif} \PY{n}{n} \PY{o}{\PYZlt{}} \PY{l+m+mi}{20}\PY{p}{:}        \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} teens}
                     \PY{n}{s} \PY{o}{+}\PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{\PYZus{}words}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{teens}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{n} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}} \PY{l+m+mi}{10}\PY{p}{]}
                 \PY{k}{elif} \PY{n}{n} \PY{o}{\PYZlt{}} \PY{l+m+mi}{100}\PY{p}{:}       \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} tens}
                     \PY{n}{m} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{n} \PY{o}{\PYZpc{}} \PY{l+m+mi}{10}

\subsection{18 Debugging}\label{debugging}}

    \textbf{1801} \texttt{Dealing\ with\ syntax\ errors}

                 \PY{k}{if} \PY{n}{h} \PY{o}{\PYZgt{}} \PY{l+m+mi}{23}\PY{p}{:} \PY{n}{h} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{o}{=} \PY{l+m+mi}{24}

                 \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} hword is the hours word)}

                 \PY{k}{if} \PY{n}{m} \PY{o+ow}{is} \PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{:}

                     \PY{k}{else}\PY{p}{:} \PY{k}{return} \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{ }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{format}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{numwords}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{h}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{\PYZus{}words}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{quarters}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{m}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{)}

         \PY{k}{class} \PY{n+nc}{saytime\PYZus{}t}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{saytime}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}   \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} wrapper for saytime to use time object}
             \PY{l+s+sd}{\PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}}
         \PY{l+s+sd}{        return the time (from a time object) as words}

Quaaaaak!
The duck has gray and white feathers.

The person takes a feather from the ground and shows it.
The dog has no quack
The dog has no feathers

The duck has no fur
The person says woof!
The person puts on a fur coat.
Arf!
The dog has white fur with black spots.

         \PY{n}{\PYZus{}\PYZus{}version\PYZus{}\PYZus{}} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{1.1.0}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}
